$(function () {
    function cheight() {
		$('.slide .container').height('');
        var maxHeight = 0;
        $('.slide .container').each(function () {            
			
				if ($(this).height() > maxHeight) {
                maxHeight = $(this).height();
				}
			
        });
        $('.slide .container').height('').height(maxHeight);
        var imgHeight = $('.mobile-image').outerHeight();
        var total = maxHeight + imgHeight;
        $('#banner-section .carousel').height('').height(total);
    }
    if ($(window).width() <= 768) {
        cheight();
    }
    $(window).resize(function () {
        if ($(window).width() <= 768) {
            cheight();
        } else {
            $('#banner-section .carousel').height('');
			$('.slide .container').height('');
        }
    });
});
</script>

        <script src="/cs/site_template/ecommerce_r/js/product-catalogue.js"></script>
        <script type="text/javascript">
            $(function() {
if($.isFunction(watchProductCatalogue))
{
                watchProductCatalogue('#productCatalogue');
}
            }); 

  

    
    function showPhones(){
  var selectedVal = $('#select-area option:selected').val();
  if(!!selectedVal){
    $('#select-area option').each(function(){
      document.getElementById($(this).val()).style.display="none";
    });
    selectedVal=$('#select-area option:selected').val();
    document.getElementById(selectedVal).style.display="block";

    $('.form-select__field').html($('#select-area option:selected').text());
  }
}
function getGeoLocatedState() {
  var state = "Kuala Lumpur";
  function calledOnGEOsuccess(p) {
    var LatLng = new google.maps.LatLng(p.coords.latitude, p.coords.longitude);
    var geocoder ;
    geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
    geocoder.geocode({'latLng': LatLng}, function(results, status)
    {
      if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK)
      {
        if (results[0])
        {
          var add= results[0].formatted_address ;
          var  value=add.split(",");
          var count=value.length;
          state = value[count-2];
   
          $('#select-area option').each(function(){
            
           
           if($.trim($(this).text().toLowerCase()) == $.trim(state.toLowerCase())){
           
            $('#select-area').val($(this).val());
            $(this).prop("selected",true);
            $('#select-area').trigger('click');
            showPhones();
          }
         });
          window.localStorage.setItem('StateName', state.toLowerCase());
        }
      }
    });
  }
  function calledinGEOFail(){
    state = "Kuala Lumpur";
    $('#select-area option').each(function(){
    if($.trim($(this).text().toLowerCase()) == $.trim(state.toLowerCase())){
   
      $('#select-area').val($(this).val());
      $(this).prop("selected",true);
      $('#select-area').trigger('click');
      showPhones();
    }
  });
  }
  if (navigator.geolocation) {
    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(calledOnGEOsuccess,calledinGEOFail);
  }
  return state;
}
window.getState = function(){
  var state = getGeoLocatedState();
 
}

</script>

            var validateCount = 5;
                $('#selectFeedbackSubject').change(function() {
                    if (($("#selectFeedbackSubject :selected").text())=="Coverage")
                    {
                        validateCount = 6;
                        var $enquiry = $('textarea#eq-text-area'),
                            $enqHtml = $("textarea#eq-text-area")[0];

                        $enquiry.remove();
                        $('.coverage-form').show();
                        $('.coverage-form').after($enqHtml);
                        $('#formType').attr('value','coverage');
                    } else {
                        $('.coverage-form').hide();
                        $('#formType').attr('value','general');
                    }
                });

                $('#feedback-countries').change(function() {
                    if (($("#feedback-countries :selected").text())=="Malaysia")
                    {
                        $('.feedback-state').show();
                    } else {

                        $('.feedback-state').hide();
                    }
                });

                function modalBodyAdjust(toggle){
                    var $body   = $('body'),
                        $zIndex = 0;
                    if(toggle === "modalUp"){
                        $body.css('overflow', 'hidden');
                        $zIndex += $('#menu--subnav').css('z-index');
                        $('#menu--subnav').slideToggle(300);
                        return;
                    }
                    if(toggle === "modalDown"){
                        $body.css('overflow', 'auto');
                        $('#menu--subnav').slideToggle(300);
                        return;
                    }
                }


               //$("#modal_trigger").leanModal({top : 100, overlay : 0.6, closeButton: ".modal_close" });
               $('.modal_trigger.custompopup').on('click',function(){
                    $('#mainPopupHolder1.custompopup').addClass('is-shown');
                    modalBodyAdjust("modalUp");

               });
               $('.modal_close.custompopup, .modal_close.custompopup').on('click',function(){
                    $('#mainPopupHolder1.custompopup').removeClass('is-shown');
                    modalBodyAdjust("modalDown");

               });

			   function checkBlank() {
					var isValid = true;
					$("#contactForm .required").each(function() {
						if($(this).is(':visible') && $(this).val().length ==0)
						{
							isValid = false;
							$(this).addClass("is-failed");
						}
						else {
							$(this).removeClass("is-failed");
						}
					});
					
					if (!isValid) {
						$(".error-feedback span").text("Please fill in all required fields.");
					}
					return isValid;
				}

						return false;
					}

	<script type="text/javascript">

	//START historic custom GATC

	// begin of constant definition
	var GA_CAT_HEADER = 'header';
	var GA_CAT_MOBILE_HEADER = 'mobile_header';
	var GA_CAT_FOOTER = 'footer';
	var GA_CAT_PRODUCT_FILTER = 'product_filter';
	var GA_CAT_LANDING_CONTENT = 'landing_content';
	var GA_CAT_TAB_HEADER = 'tab_header';
	var GA_CAT_PRE_CONTENT = 'pre_content';
	var GA_CAT_POST_CONTENT = 'post_content';
	var GA_CAT_REWARDS_TOGGLER = 'rewards_toggler';

	var GA_ACT_CLICK = 'clicked';
	var GA_ACT_SEARCH = 'search';
	// end of constant definition

	// tracking device search /*TODO	:::::	redefine category	
	function gaTrackDeviceSearch(searchParam) {		
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', GA_CAT_PRODUCT_FILTER, GA_ACT_SEARCH, document.location.href.substring(0,document.location.href.length-1)+'/?inputquery='+searchParam]);
		dataLayer.push({'event' : 'productSearch' , 'category':GA_CAT_PRODUCT_FILTER , 'label': document.location.href+'/?inputquery='+searchParam});
	}

	function gaBindATagOnClickEvent(obj, category, action) {
		
		// step: bind event to A tag
		$(obj).click(function() {
			var myObj = $(obj);
			
			return gaTrackEvent($(myObj), category, action);
			
		});

	}
	
	function gaTrackDeviceClick(productObj){
		dataLayer.push({
			'event': 'productClick',
			'ecommerce': {
				'click': {
					'actionField': {'list': 'Search Results'},
					'products': productObj
				}
			}
		});
	}
	
	function gaTrackDeviceImpression(productObj){
		dataLayer.push({
			'ecommerce': {
				'currencyCode': 'RM',
				'impressions':  productObj
			}
		});
	}

	function gaTrackEvent(obj, category, action) {

		var myObj = $(obj);
		try { 
			var label = "";
			if ($(obj).text() == '') {
				label = $(obj).attr('title');
			} else if($(obj).attr('class') != null && $(obj).attr('class').indexOf("tab_button")>=0) {
				label = $(obj).text();
			} else if($(obj).attr('class') != null && $(obj).attr('class').indexOf("banner_button")>=0) {
				var assetNameIndex = $(obj).attr('href').lastIndexOf('/');
				var assetNameEndIndex = $(obj).attr('href').indexOf('?',assetNameIndex+1);
				var assetName="";
				if(assetNameEndIndex > 0){
					assetName = $(obj).attr('href').substring(assetNameIndex+1,assetNameEndIndex);
				}else{
					assetName = $(obj).attr('href').substring(assetNameIndex+1);
				}
					label = "banner:"+assetName;
				if($(obj).attr('id') != null  && $(obj).attr('id') !='') {
					label = label+":"+$(obj).attr('id');	
				}
			} else {
				label = $(obj).text();
			}
				
			//console.info('Tracking GA event ...');
		} catch(err) {
			console.error('Unable to track GA Event.')
		}

		if ( $(myObj).attr('href') == null) {
			
		} else if( $(myObj).attr('href') == '#' ){
			//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', category, action, label]);
			dataLayer.push({'event' : action , 'category':category , 'label':label});
		}else {
			setTimeout(function() {
				dataLayer.push({'event' : action , 'category':category , 'label':label});
				
				if(myObj.attr('target') != null)
					window.open($(myObj).attr("href"));
				else
					document.location.href = $(myObj).attr('href');
				//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', category, action, label]);
			}, 100);
		}
		return false;
		
	}

	function gaPlanServiceBottomDropDownItem(obj, itemTitle) {
		return gaTrackEvent($(obj), itemTitle, GA_ACT_CLICK);
	}

	function gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass(className) {
			
		$('.' + className).find('a').each(function() {
			
			
			if ($(this).attr('class') == undefined) {
				
			} else if ($(this).attr('class').toLowerCase() == 'close_popup') {
				return;
			} else {
				
			}

			var isAlreadyBind = false;

			try {
				var myEvents = $._data($(this).get(0), 'events');
				for ( var type in myEvents) {
					//console.log($(this).text() + ' --> item:' + type);
					if (type == 'click') {
						isAlreadyBind = true;
						break;
					}
				}
			} catch (Err) {
				console.error(Err);
			}

			//console.log($(this).text() + ' --> isAlreadyBind:' + isAlreadyBind);


			if (isAlreadyBind == false) {
				var category = "n/a";
				var action = "n/a";

				if (className == 'main-nav') {
					category = GA_CAT_HEADER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}

				if (className == 'main-footer') {
					category = GA_CAT_FOOTER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}

				if (className == 'mobile-nav') {
					category = GA_CAT_MOBILE_HEADER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}
				
				if (className == 'main-small-nav') {
					category = GA_CAT_MOBILE_HEADER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}
				
				if (className == 'landing__login-panel' || className == 'landing__icon-links' || className == 'carousel') {
					category = GA_CAT_LANDING_CONTENT;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}
				
				if (className == 'tabs-holder') {
					category = GA_CAT_TAB_HEADER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}
				if (className == 'section--subnav') {
					category = GA_CAT_HEADER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}
	                       if (className == 'section--menu') {
					category = GA_CAT_HEADER;
					action = GA_ACT_CLICK;
				}
				 
				return gaBindATagOnClickEvent($(this), category, action);

			} else {
				// step: do nothing
			}
		});
	}

	function trackRewardsTogglerClick(label){
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', GA_CAT_REWARDS_TOGGLER, GA_ACT_CLICK, window.location.href ]);
		dataLayer.push({'event' : GA_ACT_CLICK , 'category':GA_CAT_REWARDS_TOGGLER , 'label': label});
	}
	
	function trackSearchForm(keyword){
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', GA_CAT_HEADER, GA_ACT_SEARCH, keyword]);
		dataLayer.push({'event' : GA_ACT_SEARCH , 'category':GA_CAT_HEADER , 'label': keyword});
	}
	
	function trackTabClick(tab_a_tag){
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', GA_CAT_TAB_HEADER, GA_ACT_CLICK, $(tab_a_tag).text()+"@"+document.location.href ]);
		dataLayer.push({'event' : GA_ACT_CLICK , 'category':GA_CAT_TAB_HEADER, 'label': $(tab_a_tag).text()+"@"+document.location.href});
	}
	
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('main-small-nav');	//top navigatio white region
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('main-nav');			//top navigation black region
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('main-footer');		//footer
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('mobile-nav');		//mobile navigation
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('landing__login-panel');		//landing page button, old is (login-panel)
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('landing__icon-links');		//landing page button
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('carousel');		//landing page banner
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('tabs-holder');		//navigation tab
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('section--subnav');
	gaBindAllATagWithEventByClass('section--menu');
	</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			function validateSiteSearchForm(form) {
				var myValue = $(form).find('input[name=keyword]').val();

				if (myValue == '') {
					return false;
				} else {
					trackSearchForm(myValue);
					return true;
				}
			}
		</script>
